msg:I have been fortunate enough to experience W hotels in some cities, and this time I stayed in room 3118, so I can offer my opinions and suggestions. First, the sound insulation of the room is not good, the sound of the aisle/the sound of the next door closing/the next door singing, etc. can be heard, which affects the experience. Second, paper towels are placed in addition to the bathroom, and it is recommended to add one to the bedside or writing desk. Third, the water temperature in the shower room fluctuates from hot to cold. It is recommended to repair or replace the constant temperature shower, but the glass door of the shower room will show dark flowers when there is hot air, and the detailed design is beautiful. Fourth, the toilet lid of the smart toilet will fail, and sometimes it will stop in the middle of opening, and it needs to be opened manually, which can be repaired. Fifth, the toiletries are complete, but the body lotion is too greasy. I have dry skin from the plateau area, and I find it very greasy and difficult to push off. Especially in a humid city like Xiamen, it is recommended to change to a moist type. body lotion. msg:Known as several luxury hotels in Xiamen, expectations are relatively high. I have stayed at Conrad Xiamen before, and there are some five-star hotels with lower prices. Compared with the w cost of 2000 per night, there is really nothing remarkable about it. It can even be said that some places are not up to the standard. Yes, not as good as a budget hotel.

The biggest problem with the hotel is hygiene. As soon as I entered the room, I saw an obvious long strand of hair on the rolled square towel on the sink, and then all kinds of dust accumulation. After boiling the kettle twice, I could pour out the powdered tea leaves or instant noodles and side dishes. s things. The carpet was also visibly dirty.

Then there is the problem of service, the attitude is very good, but the efficiency is really not good. I asked for a children's bathrobe three times, and it was delivered twice at noon and once at night. They gave us four bottles of water and even gave us bags of mineral water. What's the matter? Are you going to a farmhouse?

In the end, it may be that my aesthetics are not high enough. The style of the hotel is an ambiguous Barbie powder, which is more suitable for Internet celebrities to check in and date couples. The carpet in the room tripped me a few times, and the bed was not easy to sleep. There are too many mirrors in the room, and I am frightened by myself when I wake up in the middle of the night. Even the bathroom door is mirrored, and the front of the bathtub is also a mirror (intriguing). Our room is said to be relatively high on the 30th floor after the upgrade. When we open the window, there is a large construction site. We can see the sea in the distance. The scenery is really not good.

Oh, by the way, the air conditioner is very hot, and the whole family woke up several times at night without covering the quilt. I suspect that the temperature could not be adjusted at all (the room temperature was adjusted to 18 degrees or 24.5). When I opened the door, the corridor was cooler than the room.

The budget of the hotel may be spent on the smart toilet, which will automatically open the lid to flush and then close the lid every time it passes (a distance of one meter)... The saving grace... The Dyson hair dryer is very powerful... The children's travel wash The package is very good... The Bluetooth speakers sound good... The breakfast is delicious... But if you are staying for these, this price is not necessary. There are many, many better choices in Xiamen.

I saw a lot of families bring their children here. In fact, apart from giving meland tickets, the facilities are not friendly to children... Maybe it's closer to Baolong City... Fuling Ha takes the subway
